## pagmo.GradientsAndHessians

- Kind: class
- Summary: Native-backed wrappers over pagmo::utils::gradients_and_hessians helpers.
- Upstream reference: https://esa.github.io/pagmo2/docs/cpp/cpp_docs.html

### Methods

- `static DoubleVector EstimateGradient(problem prob, DoubleVector x, double dx)`
  - Summary: Estimates first-order gradient values for a type-erased problem.
- `static DoubleVector EstimateGradient(IProblem prob, DoubleVector x, double dx)`
  - Summary: Estimates first-order gradient values for a managed problem callback.
- `static DoubleVector EstimateGradientHighOrder(problem prob, DoubleVector x, double dx)`
  - Summary: Estimates higher-order gradient values for a type-erased problem.
- `static DoubleVector EstimateGradientHighOrder(IProblem prob, DoubleVector x, double dx)`
  - Summary: Estimates higher-order gradient values for a managed problem callback.
- `static SparsityPattern EstimateSparsity(problem prob, DoubleVector x, double dx)`
  - Summary: Estimates gradient sparsity for a type-erased problem.
- `static SparsityPattern EstimateSparsity(IProblem prob, DoubleVector x, double dx)`
  - Summary: Estimates gradient sparsity for a managed problem callback.
- `static SparsityIndex[] EstimateSparsityEntries(problem prob, DoubleVector x, double dx)`
  - Summary: Estimates gradient sparsity and projects it to managed index pairs for a type-erased problem.
- `static SparsityIndex[] EstimateSparsityEntries(IProblem prob, DoubleVector x, double dx)`
  - Summary: Estimates gradient sparsity and projects it to managed index pairs for a managed problem callback.

## pagmo.IAlgorithm

- Kind: interface
- Summary: Common managed algorithm contract across generated and handwritten algorithm wrappers.
- Upstream reference: https://esa.github.io/pagmo2/docs/cpp/cpp_docs.html

### Methods

- `IReadOnlyList<IAlgorithmLogLine> GetLogLines()`
  - Summary: Returns algorithm log lines using a child-type-agnostic shape. Algorithms that do not expose logs return an empty list.
- `population evolve(population pop)`
  - Summary: Evolves a population and returns the evolved population instance.
- `string get_extra_info()`
  - Summary: Returns additional algorithm details.
- `string get_name()`
  - Summary: Returns algorithm name.
- `uint get_seed()`
  - Summary: Returns the current random seed.
- `uint get_verbosity()`
  - Summary: Returns current verbosity level.
- `void set_seed(uint seed)`
  - Summary: Sets the random seed used by the algorithm where supported.
- `void set_verbosity(uint level)`
  - Summary: Sets verbosity level.

## pagmo.IAlgorithmLogLine

- Kind: interface
- Summary: Common projected algorithm log line contract used by .
- Upstream reference: https://esa.github.io/pagmo2/docs/cpp/cpp_docs.html

### Properties

- `string AlgorithmName { get }`
  - Summary: Gets the logical algorithm name associated with this log line.
- `IReadOnlyDictionary<string, object> RawFields { get }`
  - Summary: Gets raw field values keyed by field name for advanced/custom interpretation.

### Methods

- `string ToDisplayString()`
  - Summary: Formats the log line into a human-readable display string.

## pagmo.IProblem

- Kind: interface
- Summary: Managed problem contract for user-defined and wrapped pagmo problems.
- Upstream reference: https://esa.github.io/pagmo2/docs/cpp/cpp_docs.html

### Methods

- `DoubleVector batch_fitness(DoubleVector dvs)`
  - Summary: Evaluates fitness for a flattened batch of decision vectors when supported.
- `DoubleVector fitness(DoubleVector x)`
  - Summary: Evaluates the fitness vector at the provided decision vector.
- `PairOfDoubleVectors get_bounds()`
  - Summary: Returns lower/upper bounds for decision variables.
- `string get_extra_info()`
  - Summary: Returns additional problem metadata for diagnostics/display.
- `string get_name()`
  - Summary: Returns a human-readable problem name.
- `uint get_nec()`
  - Summary: Returns equality-constraint count.
- `uint get_nic()`
  - Summary: Returns inequality-constraint count.
- `uint get_nix()`
  - Summary: Returns number of integer decision variables.

  - Summary: Returns objective-count (f) dimension.

  - Summary: Returns thread-safety capability used by threaded pagmo execution paths.

  - Summary: Returns gradient values at the provided decision vector when supported.

  - Summary: Returns gradient sparsity pattern when supported.

  - Summary: Reports whether is implemented.

  - Summary: Reports whether is implemented.

  - Summary: Returns hessian matrices at the provided decision vector when supported.
- `VectorOfSparsityPattern hessians_sparsity()`
  - Summary: Returns hessian sparsity patterns when supported.

  - Summary: Sets the random seed when stochastic behavior supports explicit seeding.

- `ManagedProblemBase()`
  - Summary: Initializes a `ManagedProblemBase` instance.

### Methods

- `static PairOfDoubleVectors Bounds(DoubleVector lower, DoubleVector upper)`
  - Summary: Convenience helper for compact bound creation in managed UDPs.
- `static PairOfDoubleVectors Bounds(double[] lower, double[] upper)`
  - Summary: Convenience helper for compact bound creation in managed UDPs.
- `void Dispose()`
  - Summary: Releases managed resources. Override when your problem holds disposable state.
- `static VectorOfSparsityPattern HessiansSparsity(SparsityPattern[] patterns)`
  - Summary: Convenience helper for compact hessian sparsity creation in managed UDPs.
- `static SparsityPattern Sparsity(ValueTuple<uint, uint>[] entries)`
  - Summary: Convenience helper for compact gradient sparsity creation in managed UDPs.
- `static DoubleVector Vec(double[] values)`
  - Summary: Convenience helper for compact vector creation in managed UDPs.
- `DoubleVector batch_fitness(DoubleVector dvs)`
  - Summary: Evaluates flattened batch inputs when supported.
- `DoubleVector fitness(DoubleVector x)`
  - Summary: Evaluates the fitness vector at the given decision vector.
- `PairOfDoubleVectors get_bounds()`
  - Summary: Returns lower and upper decision bounds.
- `string get_extra_info()`
  - Summary: Returns additional diagnostic information.
- `string get_name()`
  - Summary: Returns a default managed problem name (the runtime type name).
- `uint get_nec()`
  - Summary: Returns equality-constraint count.
- `uint get_nic()`
  - Summary: Returns inequality-constraint count.
- `uint get_nix()`
  - Summary: Returns number of integer decision variables.
- `uint get_nobj()`
  - Summary: Returns objective-count (f) dimension.
- `int get_thread_safety()`
  - Summary: Returns thread-safety capability for threaded execution paths.
- `DoubleVector gradient(DoubleVector x)`
  - Summary: Returns gradient values when supported.
- `SparsityPattern gradient_sparsity()`
  - Summary: Returns gradient sparsity pattern when supported.
- `bool has_batch_fitness()`
  - Summary: Reports whether is implemented.
- `bool has_gradient()`
  - Summary: Reports whether is implemented.
- `bool has_gradient_sparsity()`
  - Summary: Reports whether is implemented.
- `bool has_hessians()`
  - Summary: Reports whether is implemented.
- `bool has_hessians_sparsity()`
  - Summary: Reports whether is implemented.
- `bool has_set_seed()`
  - Summary: Reports whether is implemented.
- `VectorOfVectorOfDoubles hessians(DoubleVector x)`
  - Summary: Returns hessian matrices when supported.

  - Summary: Returns hessian sparsity patterns when supported.

  - Summary: Sets the random seed for stochastic managed problems when supported.

## pagmo.grid_search

- Kind: class
- Summary: Simple exhaustive grid-search optimizer for educational and coarse-initialization scenarios. Samples each decision-variable range on a uniform grid and selects the best feasible point.
- Upstream reference: https://esa.github.io/pagmo2/docs/cpp/cpp_docs.html

### Constructors

- `grid_search(uint uniformStepsPerDimension)`
  - Summary: Creates a grid-search algorithm with one uniform step count applied to each dimension.
- `grid_search(uint[] stepsPerDimension)`
  - Summary: Creates a grid-search algorithm with per-dimension step counts.

### Methods

- `void Dispose()`
  - Summary: Disposes the managed algorithm instance.
- `population evolve(population pop)`
  - Summary: Evaluates a uniform grid and updates the population with the best feasible sampled point.
- `string get_extra_info()`
  - Summary: Returns grid configuration details.
- `string get_name()`
  - Summary: Returns the algorithm display name.
- `uint get_seed()`
  - Summary: Gets the stored algorithm seed value.
- `uint get_verbosity()`
  - Summary: Gets the current verbosity level.
- `void set_seed(uint seed)`
  - Summary: Sets the stored algorithm seed value (not used by deterministic grid enumeration).
- `void set_verbosity(uint level)`
  - Summary: Sets the verbosity level.
